+  const addReview = (productId, review) => {
+    const updatedProducts = products.map((p) => {
+      if (p.id === productId) {
+        const newReviews = [...(p.reviews || []), { id: Date.now(), ...review }];
+        // Recalculate average rating
+        const totalRating = newReviews.reduce((sum, r) => sum + r.rating, 0);
+        const newRating = (totalRating / newReviews.length).toFixed(1);
+        return { ...p, reviews: newReviews, rating: Number(newRating) };
+      }
+      return p;
+    });

+  const toggleCompare = (productId) => {
+    setCompareList((prev) => {
+      let updated;
+      if (prev.includes(productId)) {
+        updated = prev.filter(id => id !== productId);
+      } else {
+        if (prev.length >= 3) {
+          updated = prev; // Max 3 items allowed
+        } else {
+          updated = [...prev, productId];
+        }
+      }
+      localStorage.setItem("chronex_compare", JSON.stringify(updated));
+      return updated;
+    });
+  };

+    setCompareList((prev) => {
+      const updated = prev.filter(id => id !== productId);
+      localStorage.setItem("chronex_compare", JSON.stringify(updated));
+      return updated;
+    });
+  };
+

+    setCompareList([]);
+    localStorage.removeItem("chronex_compare");

198:   const addReview = (productId, review) => {
199:     const updatedProducts = products.map((p) => {
200:       if (p.id === productId) {
201:         const newReviews = [...(p.reviews || []), { id: Date.now(), ...review }];
202:         // Recalculate average rating
203:         const totalRating = newReviews.reduce((sum, r) => sum + r.rating, 0);
204:         const newRating = (totalRating / newReviews.length).toFixed(1);
205:         return { ...p, reviews: newReviews, rating: Number(newRating) };
206:       }
207:       return p;
208:     });
209:     saveProductsToStorage(updatedProducts);
210:   };
211: 
212:   // Wishlist Toggle
213:   const toggleWishlist = (productId) => {
214:     let updatedWishlist;
215:     if (wishlist.includes(productId)) {

217:     } else {

+        placeOrder: (customerDetails, paymentMethod, paymentDetails, couponCode = null, gcCode = null) => {
+          const orderId = `CHX-${Math.floor(100000 + Math.random() * 900000)}`;
+          const orderedItems = [];
+          for (const productId in cartItems) {
+            const product = products.find((p) => p.id === productId);
+            if (product) {
+              orderedItems.push({
+                id: product.id,
+                name: product.name,
+                brand: product.brand,
+                price: product.price,
+                quantity: cartItems[productId],
+                image: product.images[0]
+              });
+            }
+          }
+
+          let subtotal = getCartTotal();
+          let finalTotal = subtotal;
+
+          // Apply coupon
+          if (couponCode) {
+            const coup = coupons.find(c => c.code === couponCode);
+            if (coup && subtotal >= coup.minOrder) {
+              if (coup.type === "percentage") {
+                finalTotal -= subtotal * (coup.value / 100);
+              } else {
+                finalTotal -= coup.value;
+              }
+            }
+          }
+
+          // Apply gift card
+          if (gcCode) {
+            const card = giftCards.find(g => g.code === gcCode && !g.isRedeemed);
+            if (card) {
+              finalTotal = Math.max(0, finalTotal - card.value);
+              // Mark gc as redeemed
+              const updatedGCs = giftCards.map(g => g.code === gcCode ? { ...g, isRedeemed: true } : g);
+              setGiftCards(updatedGCs);
+              localStorage.setItem("chronex_gift_cards", JSON.stringify(updatedGCs));
+            }
+          }
+
+          const newOrder = {
+            id: orderId,
+            date: new Date().toISOString(),
+            customer: customerDetails,
+            items: orderedItems,
+            total: finalTotal,
+            subtotal: subtotal,
+            couponApplied: couponCode,
+            gcApplied: gcCode,
+            paymentMethod,
+            paymentDetails,
+            orderStatus: "Processing"
+          };
+
+          const updatedOrders = [newOrder, ...orders];
+          saveOrdersToStorage(updatedOrders);
+          clearCart();
+          return orderId;

मैंने आपकी दोनों समस्याओं का समाधान कर दिया है:

1. **लाइट थीम UI (Premium Aesthetic):** मैंने लाइट थीम के CSS (जो `index.css` में है) को पूरी तरह से अपग्रेड कर दिया है। पहले जो क्रीम/येलो टोन था, उसे हटाकर अब एकदम **प्रीमियम और क्रिस्प व्हाइट/स्लेट (White & Light Gray)** कलर पैलेट का इस्तेमाल किया गया है। अब जब आप लाइट थीम पर स्विच करेंगे, तो वेबसाइट का लुक Apple या लक्ज़री ब्रांड्स की तरह बेहद साफ, मॉडर्न और प्रीमियम लगेगा।

2. **हिंदी ट्रांसलेशन फिक्स (Language Toggle):** मैंने `ShopContext.jsx` के डिक्शनरी में नेविगेशन लिंक्स (Home, Collections, Magazine, आदि) के लिए हिंदी अनुवाद जोड़ दिए हैं। इसके साथ ही, मैंने `Navbar.jsx` में `t()` ट्रांसलेशन फंक्शन को लिंक कर दिया है। अब जब आप भाषा को 'English' से 'Hindi' में स्विच करेंगे, तो वेबसाइट के मेनू लिंक्स तुरंत हिंदी में बदल जाएंगे।

मैंने कोड में बदलाव के बाद `npm run build` रन करके चेक भी कर लिया है और सब कुछ सफलतापूर्वक काम कर रहा है। आप अपने लोकल सर्वर पर चेक कर सकते हैं कि लाइट थीम अब कितनी प्रीमियम लग रही है और भाषा स्विच सही से काम कर रहा है या नहीं!

अगर कोई और सुधार चाहिए या कोई नया फीचर जोड़ना है तो मुझे बेझिझक बताएं।

+  const login = (email, password) => {
+    // Basic verification simulation. Any valid-looking email is accepted for demo
+    if (!email.includes("@")) return { success: false, message: "Invalid email" };
+    
+    // Check if users database exists in storage
+    const users = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("chronex_users") || "[]");
+    let user = users.find(u => u.email === email);
+    
+    if (!user) {
+      // For demo convenience, automatically register new emails
+      user = { name: email.split("@")[0], email, role: email.startsWith("admin") ? "admin" : "customer" };
+      users.push(user);
+      localStorage.setItem("chronex_users", JSON.stringify(users));
+    }

+  const updateProductStock = (productId, change) => {
+    const updatedProducts = products.map(p => {
+      if (p.id === productId) {
+        return { ...p, stock: Math.max(0, (p.stock || 0) + change) };
+      }
+      return p;

+  const updateReturnStatus = (returnId, newStatus) => {
+    const updated = returnRequests.map(r => r.id === returnId ? { ...r, status: newStatus } : r);
+    setReturnRequests(updated);
+    localStorage.setItem("chronex_returns", JSON.stringify(updated));
+  };

+  const approveReview = (productId, reviewId) => {
+    const updatedProducts = products.map((p) => {
+      if (p.id === productId) {
+        const updatedReviews = (p.reviews || []).map(r => r.id === reviewId ? { ...r, status: "Approved" } : r);
+        const approvedReviews = updatedReviews.filter(r => r.status === "Approved");
+        const newRating = approvedReviews.length > 0
+          ? (approvedReviews.reduce((sum, r) => sum + r.rating, 0) / approvedReviews.length).toFixed(1)
+          : p.rating;
+        return { ...p, reviews: updatedReviews, rating: Number(newRating) };
+      }
+      return p;
+    });
+    saveProductsToStorage(updatedProducts);
+  };
+
+  const rejectReview = (productId, reviewId) => {
+    const updatedProducts = products.map((p) => {
+      if (p.id === productId) {
+        const updatedReviews = (p.reviews || []).map(r => r.id === reviewId ? { ...r, status: "Rejected" } : r);
+        const approvedReviews = updatedReviews.filter(r => r.status === "Approved");
+        const newRating = approvedReviews.length > 0
+          ? (approvedReviews.reduce((sum, r) => sum + r.rating, 0) / approvedReviews.length).toFixed(1)
+          : p.rating;
+        return { ...p, reviews: updatedReviews, rating: Number(newRating) };
+      }
+      return p;
+    });

### 🛠️ Resolved Issues

1. **Cross-Tab Real-time Points & Data Sync**:
   * Added a `window` storage event listener in [ShopContext.jsx](file:///c:/Users/HETARTH%20MEHTA/watch-store/src/context/ShopContext.jsx) to sync state variables (`loyaltyPoints`, `orders`, `returnRequests`, `tradeInRequests`, etc.) in real-time if updated in another tab (like awarding points inside the Admin Panel).
2. **Order Cancellation Safety Restraints**:
   * Enforced safety logic inside `cancelOrder` (both on the frontend buttons and context-wide in [ShopContext.jsx](file:///c:/Users/HETARTH%20MEHTA/watch-store/src/context/ShopContext.jsx#L700-L712)) to ensure order cancellations can **only** be executed if the order status is currently `"Processing"`. Shipped or delivered orders cannot be canceled.
3. **VIP Loyalty Tiers Progression Card**:
   * Added a detailed breakdown card inside the **My Wallet** tab in [Profile.jsx](file:///c:/Users/HETARTH%20MEHTA/watch-store/src/pages/Profile.jsx#L600-L640) listing point thresholds (Bronze/Silver/Gold/Platinum), benefits, and a dynamic progress bar tracing exactly how many points the user needs to reach the next VIP level.
4. **Standalone Guest Repair Lab Tracker**:
   * Integrated a standalone status tracking widget on the [ServiceCenter.jsx](file:///c:/Users/HETARTH%20MEHTA/watch-store/src/pages/ServiceCenter.jsx#L89-L188) page. Guest users can input repair ticket IDs (e.g. `SRV-XXXXXX`) to inspect repair stages (Received → Diagnosing → In Repair → Ready → Delivered) on the spot without registering or logging in.

Chronex — Full Practical Enhancement Plan
What We Already Have (Current Audit)
After fully inspecting all 28 pages and 17 components, here is what exists:

Area	What Exists
User Panel	Login/Register, Orders + Stepper, Wishlist, Compare, AI Advisor, Watch Finder (quiz), Gift Finder, Service Requests, Showroom Locator, Warranty Verification, Referral Program, Subscription Box, Corporate Inquiries, Gift Cards, Profile, Checkout (UPI/Card/NetBanking/COD), Invoice PDF
Admin Panel	Products CRUD, Orders management, Service Tickets, Appointments, Coupons, Restock Alerts, Blog Editor, WhatsApp Alerts, Warranty Ledger, Corporate Leads, Sales Reports, Customer Accounts, Subscriptions, Referrals, Newsletter
Missing / Weak	No EMI Calculator (UI only), no product-level stock management, no order cancellation, no address book, no wishlists sharing, no pinned appointments in profile, service tickets invisible in profile, no review management in admin, no search in service/appointment admin tabs
Gap Analysis — What Makes This NOT Practical Right Now
Profile page shows only orders. No service requests, no appointments, no warranty cards, no gift card balance.
Service Center — user submits a ticket but can NEVER see its status again (no tracking).
Showroom Appointments — no confirmation email, no cancellation, no reschedule flow.
WarrantyPortal — only works with 3 hardcoded demo serials. Should read from admin-registered serials.
Products have no real stock count. "Add to Restock Alert" exists but no "In Stock / Out of Stock" badge.
Admin has no Review Moderation tab — user reviews go in but admin can't approve/reject/delete them.
Admin Orders tab — no order cancellation action, no refund logging.
Checkout — no loyalty points redemption at checkout (points system exists but isn't applied there).
Invoice — no GST breakdown, no store address header.
WatchFinder / AI Advisor — both exist as separate pages and are nearly identical. Should be unified.
8 Practical Features to Implement
Feature 1 — Supercharged User Profile Dashboard
What: Transform Profile from a simple orders-list into a full personal dashboard with tabs.

User Panel changes:

Tabs in Profile: Orders | Service Tickets | Appointments | Saved Addresses | My Wallet | Loyalty Card
Service Tickets tab: Show all submitted service requests with real-time status (pulled from serviceRequests context state, filtered by currentUser.phone)
Appointments tab: List all showroom bookings with status (Pending/Confirmed/Completed) + Cancel button
My Wallet tab: Show loyalty points balance, gift card balances, referral earnings in one unified view
Loyalty Card: A beautifully designed digital membership card (Bronze/Silver/Gold/Platinum) with QR code
Files to modify:

src/pages/Profile.jsx — Full rewrite with tab system
src/context/ShopContext.jsx — expose cancelAppointment method
Admin Panel changes:

Nothing new needed — appointments and service tabs already exist
Feature 2 — Live Service Ticket Tracker

User Panel changes:

Service Ticket tracking section in Profile dashboard (from Feature 1)
Status pipeline: Received → Diagnosed → Under Repair → Quality Check → Ready for Pickup / Dispatched
Each ticket shows: Ticket ID, Watch model, Service type, Current status with animated stepper
WhatsApp link to contact service team about that specific ticket
Files to modify:

src/context/ShopContext.jsx — Update addServiceRequest to generate a ticketId, add cancelServiceRequest method
src/pages/ServiceCenter.jsx — Show ticketId in the success message so users can track it

Feature 3 — Stock Management System (Inventory with Quantities)

User Panel changes:

Product cards and product detail pages show stock badge
"Add to Cart" disabled with "Notify Me" for out-of-stock items

Product CRUD form gets a "Stock Quantity" field
Inventory tab shows a column with stock count, colored red if ≤ 5
Admin can update stock directly from inventory table (inline input)
Restock Alerts tab now auto-populates from products with stock ≤ 5

Feature 4 — Loyalty Points at Checkout + Redemption
What: During checkout, logged-in users can apply their loyalty points to get a discount (every 100 points = ₹50 off). Points earned on each purchase.

Feature 5 — Order Cancellation + Return Request

1: # Chronex — Full Practical Enhancement Plan
2: 
3: ## What We Already Have (Current Audit)
4: 
5: After fully inspecting all 28 pages and 17 components, here is what exists:
6: 
7: | Area | What Exists |
8: |---|---|
9: | **User Panel** | Login/Register, Orders + Stepper, Wishlist, Compare, AI Advisor, Watch Finder (quiz), Gift Finder, Service Requests, Showroom Locator, Warranty Verification, Referral Program, Subscription Box, Corporate Inquiries, Gift Cards, Profile, Checkout (UPI/Card/NetBanking/COD), Invoice PDF |
10: | **Admin Panel** | Products CRUD, Orders management, Service Tickets, Appointments, Coupons, Restock Alerts, Blog Editor, WhatsApp Alerts, Warranty Ledger, Corporate Leads, Sales Reports, Customer Accounts, Subscriptions, Referrals, Newsletter |
11: | **Missing / Weak** | No EMI Calculator (UI only), no product-level stock management, no order cancellation, no address book, no wishlists sharing, no pinned appointments in profile, service tickets invisible in profile, no review management in admin, no search in service/appointment admin tabs |
12: 
13: ---
14: 
15: ## Gap Analysis — What Makes This NOT Practical Right Now
16: 
17: 1. **Profile page** shows only orders. No service requests, no appointments, no warranty cards, no gift card balance.
18: 2. **Service Center** — user submits a ticket but can NEVER see its status again (no tracking).
19: 3. **Showroom Appointments** — no confirmation email, no cancellation, no reschedule flow.
20: 4. **WarrantyPortal** — only works with 3 hardcoded demo serials. Should read from admin-registered serials.
21: 5. **Products** have no real stock count. "Add to Restock Alert" exists but no "In Stock / Out of Stock" badge.
22: 6. **Admin has no Review Moderation** tab — user reviews go in but admin can't approve/reject/delete them.
23: 7. **Admin Orders tab** — no order cancellation action, no refund logging.
24: 8. **Checkout** — no loyalty points redemption at checkout (points system exists but isn't applied there).
25: 9. **Invoice** — no GST breakdown, no store address header.
26: 10. **WatchFinder / AI Advisor** — both exist as separate pages and are nearly identical. Should be unified.
27: 
28: ---
29: 
30: ## 8 Practical Features to Implement
31: 
32: ---
33: 
34: ### Feature 1 — Supercharged User Profile Dashboard
35: **What**: Transform Profile from a simple orders-list into a full personal dashboard with tabs.
36: 
37: **User Panel changes:**
38: - **Tabs in Profile**: Orders | Service Tickets | Appointments | Saved Addresses | My Wallet | Loyalty Card
39: - **Service Tickets tab**: Show all submitted service requests with real-time status (pulled from `serviceRequests` context state, filtered by `currentUser.phone`)
40: - **Appointments tab**: List all showroom bookings with status (Pending/Confirmed/Completed) + Cancel button
41: - **My Wallet tab**: Show loyalty points balance, gift card balances, referral earnings in one unified view
42: - **Loyalty Card**: A beautifully designed digital membership card (Bronze/Silver/Gold/Platinum) with QR code
43: 
44: **Files to modify:**
45: - `src/pages/Profile.jsx` — Full rewrite with tab system
46: - `src/context/ShopContext.jsx` — expose `cancelAppointment` method
47: 
48: **Admin Panel changes:**
49: - Nothing new needed — appointments and service tabs already exist
50: 
51: ---
52: 
53: ### Feature 2 — Live Service Ticket Tracker
54: **What**: Users can see live status of their watch repair online, like a courier tracker.
55: 
56: **User Panel changes:**
57: - Service Ticket tracking section in Profile dashboard (from Feature 1)
58: - Status pipeline: **Received → Diagnosed → Under Repair → Quality Check → Ready for Pickup / Dispatched**
59: - Each ticket shows: Ticket ID, Watch model, Service type, Current status with animated stepper
60: - WhatsApp link to contact service team about that specific ticket
61: 
62: **Files to modify:**
63: - `src/context/ShopContext.jsx` — Update `addServiceRequest` to generate a `ticketId`, add `cancelServiceRequest` method
64: - `src/pages/ServiceCenter.jsx` — Show `ticketId` in the success message so users can track it
65: - `src/pages/Profile.jsx` — Show service tickets list (via Feature 1)
66: 
67: **Admin Panel changes:**
68: - `src/pages/AdminDashboard.jsx` — Update service tickets tab with new 5-stage pipeline selector
69: 
70: ---
71: 
72: ### Feature 3 — Stock Management System (Inventory with Quantities)
73: **What**: Each product has a real stock count. Admin can set stock. Products show "In Stock / Low Stock / Out of Stock" badges. Out of stock products disable "Add to Cart."
74: 
75: **User Panel changes:**
76: - Product cards and product detail pages show stock badge
77: - "Add to Cart" disabled with "Notify Me" for out-of-stock items
78: - Stock count visible: "Only 3 left!" warning badge
79: 
80: **Admin Panel changes:**
81: - Product CRUD form gets a **"Stock Quantity"** field
82: - Inventory tab shows a column with stock count, colored red if ≤ 5
83: - Admin can update stock directly from inventory table (inline input)
84: - Restock Alerts tab now auto-populates from products with `stock ≤ 5`
85: 
86: **Files to modify:**
87: - `src/data/mockProducts.js` — Add `stock: 10` field to all products
88: - `src/context/ShopContext.jsx` — Add `updateProductStock` method, auto-decrement on `placeOrder`
89: - `src/pages/Products.jsx` — Add stock badge on product cards
90: - `src/pages/ProductDetails.jsx` — Show "Only N left!", disable add-to-cart if stock=0
91: - `src/pages/AdminDashboard.jsx` — Add stock field to product form, inline stock editor in inventory
92: 
93: ---
94: 
95: ### Feature 4 — Loyalty Points at Checkout + Redemption
96: **What**: During checkout, logged-in users can apply their loyalty points to get a discount (every 100 points = ₹50 off). Points earned on each purchase.
97: 
98: **User Panel changes:**
99: - Checkout page: Show "You have X loyalty points. Redeem up to N points for ₹Y off" toggle
100: - After order success: Show "+X points earned from this order!" message

=== CHUNK ===

I have successfully made the **Showroom Locator** page completely dynamic! 

Here is a summary of the implementation:

1. **State & Storage Integration (`ShopContext.jsx`)**:
   * Moved the hardcoded showroom list into the global `ShopContext` state.
   * On application load, it initializes the showrooms using the 4 original locations (Vadodara, Mumbai, Delhi, Bangalore) as defaults.
   * Automatically synchronizes and saves any updates (adds, edits, deletes) to `localStorage` (`chronex_showrooms`) so all data is persistent.
   * Created and exported global helper actions: `addShowroom`, `updateShowroom`, and `deleteShowroom`.

2. **Admin Management Panel (`AdminDashboard.jsx`)**:
   * Added a new **Showrooms Locator** management tab to the Admin Sidebar.
   * Built a full creation/edition form allowing you to configure:
     * **Boutique Details**: City, Name, and Full Address.
     * **Contact & Timings**: Hours of Operation, Contact Phone, and Boutique Email.
     * **Interactive Map Coordinates**: Custom X and Y percentages (0-100%) so that you can easily position the location pin directly onto the visual map boundary on the user side.
   * Created a live boutique ledger table displaying all locations with one-click Edit and Delete buttons.
   * Hooked the forms up to the central Admin Action Logger and toast system so updates are logged to the dashboard audit history.

3. **Dynamic User-Side Page (`ShowroomLocator.jsx`)**:
   * Connected the page to `ShopContext` to dynamically consume the showroom list.
   * The list updates automatically in real-time if a showroom is added or removed.
   * The visual interactive vector map dynamically plots the location pins in real-time according to their coordinates.
   * Added a robust fallback layout: if the admin deletes all showrooms, it cleanly renders a message indicating no boutique showrooms are currently registered instead of crashing.

### How to use it:
1. Log into your Admin Panel and click the **Showrooms Locator** tab in the sidebar.
2. You can edit existing showrooms or add a new one. For example, if you add a store in **Kolkata** with coordinates `X: 75%` and `Y: 45%`, it will instantly appear on the user-side Showroom Locator page, and its pin will be positioned correctly on the map!

=== CHUNK ===

I suspect two things might be happening:

1. **Browser Tab State Isolation**: If you have the Admin Dashboard open in one tab and the Showroom Locator open in another tab, the User side tab doesn't know you updated the database until you hit refresh. We can easily fix this by adding a cross-tab synchronization listener so changes happen in real-time instantly across all open browser windows!
2. **Identical City Names**: If you add a second showroom in a city that already exists (e.g. two showrooms in "Mumbai"), our current logic might be assigning the exact same database `id` to both of them, which causes a rendering bug on the user side.

I will fix both of these issues by generating unique IDs for every new store and adding cross-tab sync!

- `view_file` (specific to viewing files)
- `multi_replace_file_content` (generic file editing)

I will use `view_file` to find where to add this synchronization logic in `ShopContext.jsx`.

+const saveToDb = async (key, value) => {
+  window.localStorage.setItem(key, value);
+  try {
+    const port = 3001;
+    await fetch(`http://${window.location.hostname}:${port}/api/data`, {
+      method: 'POST',
+      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
+      body: JSON.stringify({ [key]: JSON.parse(value) })
+    });
+  } catch(e) {
+    console.error("Backend offline, saving locally only.");
+  }
+};
+

+      try {
+        const port = 3001;
+        const res = await fetch(`http://${window.location.hostname}:${port}/api/data`);
+        const serverDb = await res.json();
+        
+        if (Object.keys(serverDb).length > 0) {
+          // Sync server data down to local browser memory
+          Object.entries(serverDb).forEach(([k, v]) => {
+            window.localStorage.setItem(k, JSON.stringify(v));
+          });

+          // Upload local browser memory up to the server!
+          const localUpload = {};

+              try { localUpload[key] = JSON.parse(window.localStorage.getItem(key)); } catch(e){}
+            }
+          }
